Update settings.py for DRF, authentication, security\n    settings_path = f\"{PROJECT_NAME}/settings.py\"\n    with open(settings_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        settings = f.read()\n\n    # Add installed apps\n    add_apps = f\"\"\"\nINSTALLED_APPS += [\n    'rest_framework',\n    'rest_framework.authtoken',\n    '{APP_NAME}',\n    'django.contrib.staticfiles',\n]\n\"\"\"\n\n    # Add REST framework settings\n    rest_settings = \"\"\"\nREST_FRAMEWORK = {\n    'DEFAULT_AUTHENTICATION_CLASSES': [\n        'rest_framework.authentication.TokenAuthentication',\n    ],\n    'DEFAULT_PERMISSION_CLASSES': [\n        'rest_framework.permissions.IsAuthenticated',\n    ],\n}\n\"\"\"\n\n    # Add security settings\n    security_settings = \"\"\"\n# Security settings\nSECURE_SSL_REDIRECT = True\nSESSION_COOKIE_SECURE = True\nCSRF_COOKIE_SECURE = True\nX_FRAME_OPTIONS = 'DENY'\nSECURE_BROWSER_XSS_FILTER = True\nSECURE_CONTENT_TYPE_NOSNIFF = True\n\"\"\"\n\n    # Add static files\n    static_settings = \"\"\"\nSTATIC_URL = '/static/'\nSTATIC_ROOT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, 'static/')\n\"\"\"\n\n    # Add test runner\n    test_settings = \"\"\"\nTEST_RUNNER = 'django.test.runner.DiscoverRunner'\n\"\"\"\n\n    # Use SQLite for demo, you can switch to PostgreSQL for production\n    settings = settings.replace(\n        \"DATABASES = {\",\n        \"\"\"DATABASES = {\n    'default': {\n        'ENGINE': 'django.db.backends.sqlite3',\n        'NAME': BASE_DIR / 'db.sqlite3',\n    }\n\"\"\"\n    )\n\n    # Add all settings at the end of the file\n    settings += add_apps + rest_settings + security_settings + static_settings + test_settings\n\n    write_file(settings_path, settings)\n\n    # 3. Create data models (UserProfile example)\n    models_code = \"\"\"\nfrom django.db import models\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\n\nclass UserProfile(models.Model):\n    user = models.OneToOneField(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name='profile')\n    bio = models.TextField(blank=True)\n    location = models.CharField(max_length=100, blank=True)\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return f\"{self.user.username}'s profile\"\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/models.py\", models_code)\n\n    # 4. Create serializers for DRF\n    serializers_code = \"\"\"\nfrom rest_framework import serializers\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\nfrom .models import UserProfile\n\nclass UserProfileSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):\n    class Meta:\n        model = UserProfile\n        fields = ['bio', 'location']\n\nclass UserSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):\n    profile = UserProfileSerializer()\n\n    class Meta:\n        model = User\n        fields = ['id', 'username', 'email', 'profile']\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/serializers.py\", serializers_code)\n\n    # 5. Create views (DRF endpoints)\n    views_code = \"\"\"\nfrom rest_framework import generics, permissions\nfrom rest_framework.response import Response\nfrom rest_framework.views import APIView\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\nfrom .models import UserProfile\nfrom .serializers import UserSerializer, UserProfileSerializer\nfrom rest_framework.authtoken.models import Token\nfrom rest_framework.decorators import api_view, permission_classes\n\nclass UserProfileView(generics.RetrieveUpdateAPIView):\n    serializer_class = UserProfileSerializer\n    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]\n\n    def get_object(self):\n        return self.request.user.profile\n\n@api_view(['GET'])\n@permission_classes([permissions.IsAuthenticated])\ndef me(request):\n    serializer = UserSerializer(request.user)\n    return Response(serializer.data)\n\nclass RegisterView(APIView):\n    permission_classes = [permissions.AllowAny]\n\n    def post(self, request):\n        username = request.data.get('username')\n        password = request.data.get('password')\n        email = request.data.get('email', '')\n        if not username or not password:\n            return Response({'error': 'Username and password required'}, status=400)\n        if User.objects.filter(username=username).exists():\n            return Response({'error': 'Username exists'}, status=400)\n        user = User.objects.create_user(username=username, password=password, email=email)\n        UserProfile.objects.create(user=user)\n        token, created = Token.objects.get_or_create(user=user)\n        return Response({'token': token.key})\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/views.py\", views_code)\n\n    # 6. Create urls.py for the app\n    urls_code = \"\"\"\nfrom django.urls import path\nfrom .views import UserProfileView, me, RegisterView\nfrom rest_framework.authtoken.views import obtain_auth_token\n\nurlpatterns = [\n    path('profile/', UserProfileView.as_view(), name='profile'),\n    path('me/', me, name='me'),\n    path('register/', RegisterView.as_view(), name='register'),\n    path('login/', obtain_auth_token, name='login'),\n]\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/urls.py\", urls_code)\n\n    # 7. Include app urls in project urls.py\n    project_urls_path = f\"{PROJECT_NAME}/urls.py\"\n    with open(project_urls_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        project_urls = f.read()\n\n    project_urls = project_urls.replace(\n        \"from django.urls import path\",\n        \"from django.urls import path, include\"\n    )\n    project_urls = project_urls.replace(\n        \"urlpatterns = [\",\n        \"urlpatterns = [\\n    path('api/', include('myapp.urls')),\"\n    )\n    write_file(project_urls_path, project_urls)\n\n    # 8. Create basic automated tests\n    tests_code = \"\"\"\nfrom django.test import TestCase\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\nfrom rest_framework.test import APIClient\n\nclass UserTests(TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.user = User.objects.create_user(username='testuser', password='testpass')\n        self.client = APIClient()\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/login/', {'username': 'testuser', 'password': 'testpass'})\n        self.token = resp.data['token']\n        self.client.credentials(HTTP_AUTHORIZATION='Token ' + self.token)\n\n    def test_me_endpoint(self):\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/me/')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.data['username'], 'testuser')\n\n    def test_profile_update(self):\n        resp = self.client.patch('/api/profile/', {'bio': 'Hello World'})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.data['bio'], 'Hello World')\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/tests.py\", tests_code)\n\n    # 9. Migrate and create superuser instructions\n    print(\"\\nSetup complete. Now run the following commands:\")\n    print(\"python manage.py makemigrations\")\n    print(\"python manage.py migrate\")\n    print(\"python manage.py createsuperuser  # To create admin user\")\n    print(\"python manage.py test             # To run automated tests\")\n\n    # 10. Deployment guide\n    deployment_guide = \"\"\"\n==================== DEPLOYMENT GUIDE ====================\n\n1. Production Settings:\n   - Set DEBUG = False in settings.py\n   - Set ALLOWED_HOSTS = ['yourdomain.com']\n   - Use a strong SECRET_KEY (not the default)\n   - Use PostgreSQL or MySQL for production (see Django docs)\n   - Set up static files (python manage.py collectstatic)\n\n2. WSGI Server:\n   - Install gunicorn: pip install gunicorn\n   - Run: gunicorn myproject.wsgi:application --bind 0.0.0.0:8000\n\n3. Reverse Proxy:\n   - Use Nginx or Apache to proxy requests to gunicorn.\n   - Serve static files via Nginx.\n\n4. HTTPS:\n   - Use Let's Encrypt or similar for SSL certificates.\n\n5. Environment Variables:\n   - Store secrets and config in environment variables.\n\n6. Automated Tests:\n   - Run: python manage.py test\n\n7. Database Backup:\n   - Set up regular backups for your database.\n\n8. Monitoring:\n   - Use tools like Sentry, NewRelic, or server logs.\n\nFor detailed steps, see:\n- https://docs.djangoproject.com/en/4.2/howto/deployment/wsgi/\n- https://docs.djangoproject.com/en/4.2/howto/deployment/checklist/\n==========================================================\n\"\"\"\n    print(deployment_guide)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()",

Create views (DRF endpoints)\n    views_code = '''\nfrom rest_framework import generics, permissions\nfrom rest_framework.response import Response\nfrom rest_framework.views import APIView\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\nfrom .models import UserProfile\nfrom .serializers import UserSerializer, UserProfileSerializer\nfrom rest_framework.authtoken.models import Token\nfrom rest_framework.decorators import api_view, permission_classes\n\nclass UserProfileView(generics.RetrieveUpdateAPIView):\n    serializer_class = UserProfileSerializer\n    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]\n\n    def get_object(self):\n        return self.request.user.profile\n\n@api_view(['GET'])\n@permission_classes([permissions.IsAuthenticated])\ndef me(request):\n    serializer = UserSerializer(request.user)\n    return Response(serializer.data)\n\nclass RegisterView(APIView):\n    permission_classes = [permissions.AllowAny]\n\n    def post(self, request):\n        username = request.data.get('username')\n        password = request.data.get('password')\n        email = request.data.get('email', '')\n        if not username or not password:\n            return Response({'error': 'Username and password required'}, status=400)\n        if User.objects.filter(username=username).exists():\n            return Response({'error': 'Username exists'}, status=400)\n        user = User.objects.create_user(username=username, password=password, email=email)\n        UserProfile.objects.create(user=user)\n        token, created = Token.objects.get_or_create(user=user)\n        return Response({'token': token.key})\n'''\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/views.py\", views_code)\n\n    # 6. Create serializers for DRF\n    serializers_code = \"\"\"\nfrom rest_framework import serializers\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\nfrom .models import UserProfile\n\nclass UserProfileSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):\n    class Meta:\n        model = UserProfile\n        fields = ['bio', 'location']\n\nclass UserSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):\n    profile = UserProfileSerializer()\n\n    class Meta:\n        model = User\n        fields = ['id', 'username', 'email', 'profile']\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/serializers.py\", serializers_code)\n\n    # 5. Create views (DRF endpoints)\n    views_code = \"\"\"\nfrom rest_framework import generics, permissions\nfrom rest_framework.response import Response\nfrom rest_framework.views import APIView\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\nfrom .models import UserProfile\nfrom .serializers import UserSerializer, UserProfileSerializer\nfrom rest_framework.authtoken.models import Token\nfrom rest_framework.decorators import api_view, permission_classes\n\nclass UserProfileView(generics.RetrieveUpdateAPIView):\n    serializer_class = UserProfileSerializer\n    permission_classes = [permissions.IsAuthenticated]\n\n    def get_object(self):\n        return self.request.user.profile\n\n@api_view(['GET'])\n@permission_classes([permissions.IsAuthenticated])\ndef me(request):\n    serializer = UserSerializer(request.user)\n    return Response(serializer.data)\n\nclass RegisterView(APIView):\n    permission_classes = [permissions.AllowAny]\n\n    def post(self, request):\n        username = request.data.get('username')\n        password = request.data.get('password')\n        email = request.data.get('email', '')\n        if not username or not password:\n            return Response({'error': 'Username and password required'}, status=400)\n        if User.objects.filter(username=username).exists():\n            return Response({'error': 'Username exists'}, status=400)\n        user = User.objects.create_user(username=username, password=password, email=email)\n        UserProfile.objects.create(user=user)\n        token, created = Token.objects.get_or_create(user=user)\n        return Response({'token': token.key})\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/views.py\", views_code)\n\n    # 6. Create urls.py for the app\n    urls_code = \"\"\"\nfrom django.urls import path\nfrom .views import UserProfileView, me, RegisterView\nfrom rest_framework.authtoken.views import obtain_auth_token\n\nurlpatterns = [\n    path('profile/', UserProfileView.as_view(), name='profile'),\n    path('me/', me, name='me'),\n    path('register/', RegisterView.as_view(), name='register'),\n    path('login/', obtain_auth_token, name='login'),\n]\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/urls.py\", urls_code)\n\n    # 7. Create basic automated tests\n    tests_code = \"\"\"\nfrom django.test import TestCase\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\nfrom rest_framework.test import APIClient\n\nclass UserTests(TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.user = User.objects.create_user(username='testuser', password='testpass')\n        self.client = APIClient()\n        resp = self.client.post('/api/login/', {'username': 'testuser', 'password': 'testpass'})\n        self.token = resp.data['token']\n        self.client.credentials(HTTP_AUTHORIZATION='Token ' + self.token)\n\n    def test_me_endpoint(self):\n        resp = self.client.get('/api/me/')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.data['username'], 'testuser')\n\n    def test_profile_update(self):\n        resp = self.client.patch('/api/profile/', {'bio': 'Hello World'})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.data['bio'], 'Hello World')\n\"\"\"\n    write_file(f\"{APP_NAME}/tests.py\", tests_code)\n\n    # 9. Check that views.py defines UserProfileView, me, RegisterView\n        views_content = files_written[f\"{APP_NAME}/views.py\"]\n        self.assertIn(\"class UserProfileView\", views_content)\n        self.assertIn(\"def me(request):\", views_content)\n        self.assertIn(\"class RegisterView\", views_content)\n\n        # Check that urls.py includes all endpoints\n        urls_content = files_written[f\"{APP_NAME}/urls.py\"]\n        for endpoint in [\"profile/\", \"me/\", \"register/\", \"login/\", \"token/refresh/\", \"token/verify/\"]:\n            self.assertIn(f\"path('{endpoint}\", urls_content)\n\n        # Check that tests.py contains test cases for endpoints\n        tests_content = files_written[f\"{APP_NAME}/tests.py\"]\n        for test in [\"test_me_endpoint\", \"test_profile_update\", \"test_register\"]:\n            self.assertIn(test, tests_content)\n\n    def test_edge_case_settings_patch(self):\n        # Test that the settings patch does not break if DATABASES is missing\n        settings = \"SOME_SETTING = True\\n\"\n        # Should not raise\n        patched = settings.replace(\n            \"DATABASES = {\",\n            \"\"\"DATABASES = {\n    'default': {\n        'ENGINE': 'django.db.backends.sqlite3',\n        'NAME': BASE_DIR / 'db.sqlite3',\n    }\n\"\"\"\n        )\n        self.assertNotIn(\"'ENGINE': 'django.db.backends.sqlite3'\", patched)\n        # Should not raise SyntaxError\n        compile(models_code, \"<models.py>\", \"exec\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    unittest.main()",
